{
  role: 'assistant',
  content: null,
  function_call: {
    name: 'python',
    arguments: 'import nltk\n' +
      'from nltk.tokenize import word_tokenize, sent_tokenize\n' +
      'from nltk.corpus import stopwords\n' +
      'from nltk.probability import FreqDist\n' +
      'from nltk.sentiment import SentimentIntensityAnalyzer\n' +
      'import string\n' +
      '\n' +
      'def analyze_report(report):\n' +
      '    # Tokenize the report into sentences\n' +
      '    report_sentences = sent_tokenize(report)\n' +
      '\n' +
      '    # Tokenize the report into words\n' +
      '    report_words = word_tokenize(report)\n' +
      '\n' +
      '    # Remove stopwords and punctuation\n' +
      '    stop_words = set(stopwords.words("english"))\n' +
      '    report_words_cleaned = [word.lower() for word in report_words if word.lower() not in stop_words and word not in string.punctuation]\n' +
      '\n' +
      '    # Calculate word frequency\n' +
      '    word_freq = FreqDist(report_words_cleaned)\n' +
      '\n' +
      '    # Calculate sentiment score\n' +
      '    sia = SentimentIntensityAnalyzer()\n' +
      "    sentiment_score = sia.polarity_scores(report)['compound']\n" +
      '\n' +
      '    # Return results\n' +
      '    return {\n' +
      '        "sentences": report_sentences,\n' +
      '        "word_frequency": dict(word_freq),\n' +
      '        "sentiment_score": sentiment_score\n' +
      '    }\n' +
      '\n' +
      'report = "hmm hmm hmm hmm hmm"\n' +
      'analysis = analyze_report(report)\n' +
      'analysis'
  }
}
